## Executed Plan
1. Navigate to `http://localhost:5173/` → heading "Kindling Test App", 4 nav links (About, Contact, /health, /ping), sections "Pages" and "API Endpoints" -- **PASS**
2. Navigate to `http://localhost:5173/about` via full page reload → heading "About", sections "What this is" and "Pages", descriptive paragraph confirmed in body text -- **PASS**
3. Navigate to `http://localhost:5173/contact` → heading "Contact Us", 2 inputs + 1 textarea, button "Send Message", labels Name/Email/Message -- **PASS**
4. Submit empty contact form → all three "is required" errors ("Name is required", "Email is required", "Message is required") appear; all three fields show `rgb(255, 0, 0)` red border -- **PASS**
5. Fill name+message, enter invalid email "not-an-email" → "Please enter a valid email" error appears; no other errors -- **PASS**
6. Fill valid name/email/message → heading changes to "Thank you!", confirmation text "Your message has been received. We'll get back to you soon." -- **PASS**
7. Click "Back to home" from success state → URL changes to `http://localhost:5173/`, heading "Kindling Test App" confirmed after navigation -- **PASS**
8. Full SSR verification at `/about` via direct URL → heading "About", body text confirms descriptive content about the test application rendering correctly -- **PASS**

## Proof of Work
**Setup**: Dev server confirmed running on port 5173. Playwright eval server started on port 9222 with `--video-dir` and `--screenshot-dir` pointing to the proof workspace. Screenshot and video directories confirmed created.

**Home page verification**: `page.goto("http://localhost:5173/")` with `networkidle` wait. Heading "Kindling Test App" confirmed. Nav links array: `["About","Contact","/health","/ping"]`. Sections: `["Pages","API Endpoints"]`. Screenshot captured.

**About page verification**: `page.goto("http://localhost:5173/about")`. Heading "About" confirmed. Sections `["What this is","Pages"]` confirmed. Body text includes descriptive paragraph: "This is a minimal RedwoodSDK application used as a test target for kindling's verification system." Screenshot captured.

**Contact form layout**: Heading "Contact Us" confirmed. 2 inputs, 1 textarea, 1 button, 3 labels (Name, Email, Message) confirmed via DOM query. Screenshot captured.

**Empty form validation**: After `click("button[type=submit]")` with all empty fields, form text includes all three "is required" errors. All three field elements have `rgb(255, 0, 0)` border color (red). Screenshot captured.

**Invalid email validation**: After filling name="Alice", message="Hello world", email="not-an-email" and submitting, form text shows only "Please enter a valid email" — no "required" errors. Screenshot captured.

**Valid submission**: After filling valid data and submitting, heading changes to "Thank you!" and body shows "Your message has been received. We'll get back to you soon." Screenshot captured.

**Back-to-home navigation**: After clicking "Back to home" on success state, `page.url()` returns `http://localhost:5173/` and heading "Kindling Test App" confirmed after wait. Screenshot captured.

**Eval server close**: `POST /close` finalized both WebM video files. Total 2 video files (1.4 MB and 2.9 MB) confirmed present on disk.
